<p><b>Riyad Karim Mahrez</b> (<a href="/wiki/Arabic_language" class="mw-redirect" title="Arabic language">Arabic</a>: <span lang="ar" dir="rtl">  </span>&#8206;, <small><a href="/wiki/Romanization_of_Arabic" title="Romanization of Arabic">romanized</a>:&#160;</small><i lang="ar-Latn" title="Arabic-language romanization">Riy Karm Maraz</i>; born 21 February 1991) is a professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Winger" title="Midfielder">winger</a> for <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> club <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City</a> and captains the <a href="/wiki/Algeria_national_football_team" title="Algeria national football team">Algerian national team</a>.
</p><p>Mahrez began his career as a youth player for French club AAS Sarcelles. He turned professional in 2009 with <a href="/wiki/Quimper_Kerfeunteun_F.C." title="Quimper Kerfeunteun F.C.">Quimper</a>, where he played for only one season before moving to <a href="/wiki/Le_Havre_AC" title="Le Havre AC">Le Havre</a>, spending a total of three years with them, initially playing for their reserve team and then becoming a first-team regular. In January 2014, Mahrez signed for English side <a href="/wiki/Leicester_City_F.C." title="Leicester City F.C.">Leicester City</a>, helping them win the <a href="/wiki/EFL_Championship" title="EFL Championship">Championship</a> and promotion to the Premier League at the end of his first season. In the 201516 season he was the <a href="/wiki/Algerian_Footballer_of_the_Year" title="Algerian Footballer of the Year">Algerian Footballer of the Year</a>, the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Players%27_Player_of_the_Year" title="PFA Players&#39; Player of the Year">PFA Players' Player of the Year</a>, and was a member of the Premier League <a href="/wiki/PFA_Team_of_the_Year" title="PFA Team of the Year">PFA Team of the Year</a> as he helped Leicester City win the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Premier_League" title="201516 Premier League">Premier League</a>. He signed for Manchester City in 2018, winning the Premier League, <a href="/wiki/FA_Cup" title="FA Cup">FA Cup</a> and <a href="/wiki/EFL_Cup" title="EFL Cup">EFL Cup</a> in his first season.
</p><p>Born in France, Mahrez made his international debut for <a href="/wiki/Algeria_national_football_team" title="Algeria national football team">Algeria</a> in 2014 and represented them at the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 FIFA World Cup</a> and at the <a href="/wiki/2015_Africa_Cup_of_Nations" title="2015 Africa Cup of Nations">2015</a>, <a href="/wiki/2017_Africa_Cup_of_Nations" title="2017 Africa Cup of Nations">2017</a> and <a href="/wiki/2019_Africa_Cup_of_Nations" title="2019 Africa Cup of Nations">2019</a> <a href="/wiki/Africa_Cup_of_Nations" title="Africa Cup of Nations">Africa Cup of Nations</a>, winning the African Cup of Nations in 2019. In 2016 he was named <a href="/wiki/Confederation_of_African_Football" title="Confederation of African Football">CAF</a>'s <a href="/wiki/African_Footballer_of_the_Year" title="African Footballer of the Year">African Footballer of the Year</a>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life">Early life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Riyad_Mahrez&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Early life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Mahrez was born in <a href="/wiki/Sarcelles" title="Sarcelles">Sarcelles</a>, France, to an Algerian father and a mother of Algerian and Moroccan descent.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> His father Ahmed was from <a href="/wiki/Beni_Snous" title="Beni Snous">Beni Snous</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tlemcen_District" class="mw-redirect" title="Tlemcen District">Tlemcen District</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> Growing up, Mahrez would regularly spend his holidays in Algeria.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-doyle_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-doyle-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> His childhood friends included fellow footballers such as <a href="/wiki/Wissam_Ben_Yedder" title="Wissam Ben Yedder">Wissam Ben Yedder</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Mahrez's father had played football in Algeria.<sup id="cite_ref-doyle_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-doyle-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> When Mahrez was fifteen, his father died of a heart attack. He reflected that "I don't know if I started to be more serious but after the death of my dad things started to go for me. Maybe in my head, I wanted it more".<sup id="cite_ref-doyle_7-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-doyle-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Riyad_Mahrez&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Club career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_career">Early career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Riyad_Mahrez&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Early career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Although often overlooked by teams due to his slender build, Mahrez developed ball skills that brought him attention.<sup id="cite_ref-doyle_7-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-doyle-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He joined AAS Sarcelles in 2004.<sup id="cite_ref-journey_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-journey-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In 2009, Mahrez joined <a href="/wiki/Championnat_de_France_amateur" class="mw-redirect" title="Championnat de France amateur">CFA</a> side <a href="/wiki/Quimper_Kerfeunteun_F.C." title="Quimper Kerfeunteun F.C.">Quimper</a> from AAS Sarcelles, making 22 appearances and scoring 2 goals in his first season with the club.<sup id="cite_ref-Quimper_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Quimper-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> While playing for Quimper he lived with <a href="/wiki/Mathias_Pogba" title="Mathias Pogba">Mathias Pogba</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-journey_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-journey-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He joined <a href="/wiki/Le_Havre_AC" title="Le Havre AC">Le Havre</a> in 2010, turning down offers from leading French teams <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain" class="mw-redirect" title="Paris Saint-Germain">Paris Saint-Germain</a> and <a href="/wiki/Olympique_de_Marseille" title="Olympique de Marseille">Marseille</a> to join them, being enticed by their youth system.<sup id="cite_ref-doyle_7-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-doyle-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> He initially played for their reserve team, Le Havre II, before going on to play 60 times and score 6 goals for the first team in the French <a href="/wiki/Ligue_2" title="Ligue 2">Ligue 2</a> from 2011 until leaving in January 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-SW_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SW-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> He criticised Ligue 2 for what he saw as a reliance on defence and teams aiming for a goalless draw in every match.<sup id="cite_ref-doyle_7-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-doyle-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Leicester_City">Leicester City</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Riyad_Mahrez&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Leicester City">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Riyad_Mahrez.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Riyad_Mahrez.jpg/220px-Riyad_Mahrez.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="326" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Riyad_Mahrez.jpg/330px-Riyad_Mahrez.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Riyad_Mahrez.jpg/440px-Riyad_Mahrez.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1325" data-file-height="1966" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Riyad_Mahrez.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Mahrez playing for Leicester in 2014</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:305px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Mahrez_free_kick_1_(16476351346).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Mahrez_free_kick_1_%2816476351346%29.jpg/303px-Mahrez_free_kick_1_%2816476351346%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="303" height="202" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Mahrez_free_kick_1_%2816476351346%29.jpg/455px-Mahrez_free_kick_1_%2816476351346%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Mahrez_free_kick_1_%2816476351346%29.jpg/606px-Mahrez_free_kick_1_%2816476351346%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4570" data-file-height="3045" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Mahrez_free_kick_1_(16476351346).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Mahrez taking a free kick away to <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a> in February 2015.</div></div></div>
<h4><span id="2013.E2.80.9314_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201314_season">201314 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Riyad_Mahrez&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: 201314 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>While Mahrez was playing for Le Havre, English <a href="/wiki/EFL_Championship" title="EFL Championship">Championship</a> club <a href="/wiki/Leicester_City_F.C." title="Leicester City F.C.">Leicester City</a>'s scout <a href="/wiki/Steve_Walsh_(scout)" title="Steve Walsh (scout)">Steve Walsh</a> was monitoring teammate <a href="/wiki/Ryan_Mendes" title="Ryan Mendes">Ryan Mendes</a>, but was instead impressed by Mahrez.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> Mahrez had never heard of Leicester, whom he initially presumed to be a rugby club.<sup id="cite_ref-street_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-street-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> On 11 January 2014, he signed a three-and-a-half-year contract.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> His friends and family were initially sceptical of a move to English football due to its physical nature, believing that his style of play would be more suited to Spain.<sup id="cite_ref-doyle_7-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-doyle-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Mahrez made his debut on 25 January 2014, coming on in the 79th minute as a substitute replacing fellow winger <a href="/wiki/Lloyd_Dyer" title="Lloyd Dyer">Lloyd Dyer</a>, in the 20 win against <a href="/wiki/Middlesbrough_F.C." title="Middlesbrough F.C.">Middlesbrough</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> After making four substitute appearances for Leicester, including scoring his first goal for the club, an 82nd-minute equaliser against <a href="/wiki/Leicester_City_F.C.%E2%80%93Nottingham_Forest_F.C._rivalry" title="Leicester City F.C.Nottingham Forest F.C. rivalry">local rivals</a> <a href="/wiki/Nottingham_Forest_F.C." title="Nottingham Forest F.C.">Nottingham Forest</a>, manager Nigel Pearson announced in February 2014 that he thought Mahrez was ready to start games.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> Leicester ended <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_Football_League_Championship" title="201314 Football League Championship">the season</a> as winners of the Championship, returning to the Premier League for the first time in ten years.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2014.E2.80.9315_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201415_season">201415 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Riyad_Mahrez&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: 201415 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Mahrez made his Premier League debut on 16 August 2014, and scored his first goal in the division on 4 October 2014 in a 22 draw with <a href="/wiki/Burnley_F.C." title="Burnley F.C.">Burnley</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-SB_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SB-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> Mahrez was part of the Leicester team that won seven of its final nine matches of the season to avoid relegation to the Football League. He scored both goals in a 20 defeat of <a href="/wiki/Southampton_F.C." title="Southampton F.C.">Southampton</a> on 9 May<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> and ended <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_Leicester_City_F.C._season" title="201415 Leicester City F.C. season">the season</a> with four goals and three assists from 30 appearances.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2015.E2.80.9316_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201516_season">201516 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Riyad_Mahrez&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 201516 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>He signed a new four-year contract with Leicester in August 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> On 8 August 2015, Mahrez scored two goals in the season opener against <a href="/wiki/Sunderland_A.F.C." title="Sunderland A.F.C.">Sunderland</a> in a 42 home win.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> He was later described as the club's "match winner" by captain <a href="/wiki/Wes_Morgan" title="Wes Morgan">Wes Morgan</a>, following "superb form" which saw him score four goals in the first three games of the season.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After scoring four goals in the opening four games of the 201516 season, Mahrez was nominated for the <a href="/wiki/Premier_League_Player_of_the_Month" title="Premier League Player of the Month">Premier League Player of the Month</a> award.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> By 3 November 2015, he had scored seven goals in 10 Premier League games.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> On 5 December, Mahrez scored a hat-trick as Leicester defeated <a href="/wiki/Swansea_City_F.C." class="mw-redirect" title="Swansea City F.C.">Swansea City</a> 30 to go top of the Premier League, putting him on ten league goals for the season and making him the first Algerian to score a <a href="/wiki/List_of_Premier_League_hat-tricks" title="List of Premier League hat-tricks">Premier League hat-trick</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> Mahrez and his midfield partners <a href="/wiki/Marc_Albrighton" title="Marc Albrighton">Marc Albrighton</a>, <a href="/wiki/N%27Golo_Kant%C3%A9" title="N&#39;Golo Kanté">N'Golo Kanté</a> and <a href="/wiki/Danny_Drinkwater" title="Danny Drinkwater">Danny Drinkwater</a> received plaudits for their part in Leicester's early season run of form,<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> and manager <a href="/wiki/Claudio_Ranieri" title="Claudio Ranieri">Claudio Ranieri</a> described Mahrez and forward <a href="/wiki/Jamie_Vardy" title="Jamie Vardy">Jamie Vardy</a> as "priceless" ahead of the January transfer window.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In January 2016 Mahrez's transfer value was said to have risen from £4.5 million to £30.1 million, ranking him among the top 50 most valuable players in Europe.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> In the same year, Mahrez's popularity in his homeland led Leicester to have over almost three times as many <a href="/wiki/Facebook" title="Facebook">Facebook</a> fans in Algeria than in the UK.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> The barbershop in Sarcelles that he frequented from his childhood became a destination for fans from as far as Belgium, desiring the same haircut.<sup id="cite_ref-journey_9-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-journey-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Mahrez was one of four Leicester players named in the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Team_of_the_Year" title="PFA Team of the Year">PFA Team of the Year</a> in April 2016,<sup id="cite_ref-PFATeam_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PFATeam-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> and later that month he won the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Players%27_Player_of_the_Year" title="PFA Players&#39; Player of the Year">PFA Players' Player of the Year</a> award.<sup id="cite_ref-PFAPlayer_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PFAPlayer-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> He was the first African to earn the accolade.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> When Leicester finished the season as champions, Mahrez became the first Algerian to win a Premier League medal.<sup id="cite_ref-PL_37-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PL-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2016.E2.80.9317_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201617_season">201617 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Riyad_Mahrez&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: 201617 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:35%; ;"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1012376600">.mw-parser-output .quotebox{background-color:#F9F9F9;border:1px solid #aaa;box-sizing:border-box;padding:10px;font-size:88%;max-width:100%}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft{margin:0.5em 1.4em 0.8em 0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright{margin:0.5em 0 0.8em 1.4em}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.centered{margin:0.5em auto 0.8em auto}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft p,.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright p{font-style:inherit}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-title{background-color:#F9F9F9;text-align:center;font-size:larger;font-weight:bold}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:before{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:"  ";vertical-align:-45%;line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:after{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:"  ";line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .left-aligned{text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .right-aligned{text-align:right}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .center-aligned{text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .quotebox cite{display:block;font-style:normal}@media screen and (max-width:640px){.mw-parser-output .quotebox{width:100%!important;margin:0 0 0.8em!important;float:none!important}}</style>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">I am fiercely ambitious and feel now is the time to move on to a new experience. I've always enjoyed a good relationship with the chairman and everyone at the club, and I hope I have been able to repay the faith shown to me by my performances and commitment on the pitch during my time here.</div>
<p><cite class="right-aligned" style=""> Mahrez speaking to <i><a href="/wiki/The_Guardian" title="The Guardian">The Guardian</a></i> about his desire to leave Leicester City.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>He signed a new four-year contract with Leicester in August 2016.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> He was nominated for the <a href="/wiki/2016_Ballon_d%27Or" title="2016 Ballon d&#39;Or">Ballon d'Or</a> in October 2016,<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> finishing seventh.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> He won the <a href="/wiki/BBC_African_Footballer_of_the_Year" title="BBC African Footballer of the Year">BBC African Footballer of the Year</a> award in December 2016.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCAfrican_42-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCAfrican-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Mahrez did not offer a big season especially with the decline in the level of Leicester, but helped the team's arrival in the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_UEFA_Champions_League#Quarter-finals" title="201617 UEFA Champions League">quarter-finals of the Champions League</a> for the first time, scoring four goals and two assists.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> On 6 May, Mahrez played his 100th Premier League game for Leicester, against <a href="/wiki/Watford_F.C." title="Watford F.C.">Watford</a>, scoring in the process.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2017.E2.80.9318_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201718_season">201718 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Riyad_Mahrez&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: 201718 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>At the end of the 201617 season, Mahrez announced that he wished to leave the club.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> Following the announcement, <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a> manager <a href="/wiki/Ars%C3%A8ne_Wenger" title="Arsène Wenger">Arsène Wenger</a> stated his interest in signing Mahrez,<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> and Italian side <a href="/wiki/A.S._Roma" title="A.S. Roma">Roma</a> had a bid for Mahrez rejected in July 2017.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> In August 2017 he spoke of his "focus" despite his uncertain future at the club.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Algerian_Football_Federation" title="Algerian Football Federation">Algerian Football Federation</a> reported on 31 August, the last day of the transfer window, that it had allowed him to leave the national team and travel quickly to Europe in order to complete his transfer to an interested club; this transfer did not materialise.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> In January 2018 he again asked for a transfer away from the club.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> After a move to <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City</a> fell through,<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> Mahrez stopped attending training at Leicester.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> His behaviour was criticised by commentator and former player <a href="/wiki/Chris_Sutton" title="Chris Sutton">Chris Sutton</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> Mahrez was critical about the "untrue assumptions" about his absence from the team,<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> and later thanked his teammates for their support.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Manchester_City">Manchester City</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Riyad_Mahrez&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Manchester City">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="2018.E2.80.9319_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201819_season">201819 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Riyad_Mahrez&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: 201819 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 10 July 2018, <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City</a> confirmed the signing of Mahrez on a five-year contract. The transfer fee of £60m made Mahrez the <a href="/wiki/List_of_most_expensive_association_football_transfers" title="List of most expensive association football transfers">most expensive African footballer</a>, and also Manchester City's most expensive signing and a record transfer fee received by <a href="/wiki/Leicester_City_F.C." title="Leicester City F.C.">Leicester City</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> He stated he wanted to win the Champions League with the club.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> He made his debut as a starter on 5 August, as City defeated Chelsea 20 to win the <a href="/wiki/2018_FA_Community_Shield" title="2018 FA Community Shield">2018 FA Community Shield</a> at <a href="/wiki/Wembley_Stadium" title="Wembley Stadium">Wembley Stadium</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-shield_62-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-shield-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> On 22 September 2018, coming on as a substitute in the 61st minute Mahrez scored a brace for Citizens against <a href="/wiki/Cardiff_City_F.C." title="Cardiff City F.C.">Cardiff City</a>, The first goal was his first with Manchester City.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 29 October 2018, Mahrez scored the only goal for Manchester City in a 10 away victory against <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham Hotspur</a>. He dedicated the goal to <a href="/wiki/Vichai_Srivaddhanaprabha" title="Vichai Srivaddhanaprabha">Vichai Srivaddhanaprabha</a>, the former owner of his previous club Leicester City, who had recently <a href="/wiki/2018_Leicester_City_F.C._helicopter_crash" class="mw-redirect" title="2018 Leicester City F.C. helicopter crash">died in a helicopter crash</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> On 24 February 2019, Mahrez won his second title with Manchester City by winning the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_EFL_Cup" title="201819 EFL Cup">EFL Cup</a> against <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a>, also won the best player of the EFL Cup although he did not participate in the final.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At the end of his first season with Manchester City, despite having "limited playing time" (including just 14 league starts),<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> Mahrez won the Premier League title for the second time, and his first with Manchester City, becoming the second African player to win the title with two different clubs after <a href="/wiki/Kolo_Tour%C3%A9" title="Kolo Touré">Kolo Touré</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> Mahrez said he would not leave City despite his lack of game time, claiming that he knew his first season would be difficult and he had come to a stable team with good players but he trusted his potential.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> A week after in the FA Cup final, he achieved his fourth title of the season after beating <a href="/wiki/Watford_F.C." title="Watford F.C.">Watford</a> 60 becoming the first African player to complete an English domestic <a href="/wiki/Treble_(association_football)" title="Treble (association football)">treble</a>, as he earlier won the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_EFL_Cup" title="201819 EFL Cup">201819 EFL Cup</a> and the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_Premier_League" title="201819 Premier League">201819 Premier League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2019.E2.80.9320_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201920_season">201920 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Riyad_Mahrez&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: 201920 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>In August 2019, Mahrez missed the <a href="/wiki/2019_FA_Community_Shield" title="2019 FA Community Shield">2019 FA Community Shield</a> over concerns about medicine he had been given by the Algerian national team.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> The Algerian FA described it as a "non-event".<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> Mahrez later started in Manchester City's 50 opening day away win against <a href="/wiki/West_Ham_United_F.C." title="West Ham United F.C.">West Ham United</a>, being involved in all 5 of his side's goals, providing two assists for hat-trick scorer <a href="/wiki/Raheem_Sterling" title="Raheem Sterling">Raheem Sterling</a> and winning a penalty for <a href="/wiki/Sergio_Ag%C3%BCero" title="Sergio Agüero">Sergio Agüero</a> to eventually score after a retake.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2020.E2.80.9321_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="202021_season">202021 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Riyad_Mahrez&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: 202021 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 28 November 2020, Mahrez scored his first hat-trick for City in a 50 home win over <a href="/wiki/Burnley_F.C." title="Burnley F.C.">Burnley</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Riyad_Mahrez&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: International career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:200px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Riyad_Mahrez_-_2014_World_Cup.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/bb/Riyad_Mahrez_-_2014_World_Cup.jpg" decoding="async" width="198" height="295" class="thumbimage" data-file-width="198" data-file-height="295" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Riyad_Mahrez_-_2014_World_Cup.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Mahrez playing for <a href="/wiki/Algeria_national_football_team" title="Algeria national football team">Algeria</a> against <a href="/wiki/Belgium_national_football_team" title="Belgium national football team">Belgium</a> at the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 FIFA World Cup</a>.</div></div></div>
<p>In November 2013, French-born Mahrez expressed his desire to represent <a href="/wiki/Algeria_national_football_team" title="Algeria national football team">Algeria</a> internationally.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> He was called up to the provisional Algeria squad for the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 FIFA World Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> On 31 May 2014, Mahrez made his international debut for the <i>Desert Foxes</i> as a starter in a pre-World Cup friendly match against <a href="/wiki/Armenia_national_football_team" title="Armenia national football team">Armenia</a>, and he was subsequently called up to the full squad for the tournament on 2 June.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> The Algerian media were critical of his inclusion and alleged that he had paid manager <a href="/wiki/Vahid_Halilhod%C5%BEi%C4%87" title="Vahid Halilhodi">Vahid Halilhodi</a> for a place in the squad.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-msn_80-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-msn-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup> Mahrez played in the opening group game against <a href="/wiki/Belgium_national_football_team" title="Belgium national football team">Belgium</a>, then was dropped for the remainder of the tournament, in which Algeria reached the last 16.<sup id="cite_ref-msn_80-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-msn-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 15 October 2014, Mahrez scored his first international goal, as well as setting up <a href="/wiki/Islam_Slimani" title="Islam Slimani">Islam Slimani</a> in Algeria's 30, <a href="/wiki/2015_Africa_Cup_of_Nations_qualification" title="2015 Africa Cup of Nations qualification">Africa Cup of Nations</a> qualifier against <a href="/wiki/Malawi_national_football_team" title="Malawi national football team">Malawi</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> In December 2014 he was announced as a member of Algeria's squad for the <a href="/wiki/2015_Africa_Cup_of_Nations" title="2015 Africa Cup of Nations">final tournament in Equatorial Guinea</a> for the first time.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> his first meeting was against <a href="/wiki/South_Africa_national_football_team" title="South Africa national football team">South Africa</a> where he participated in the 60 minutes before the change in the second throw against <a href="/wiki/Ghana_national_football_team" title="Ghana national football team">Ghana</a> substitute in the last 20 minutes where the Algerian team were defeated by a single goal in their last game in the <a href="/wiki/2015_Africa_Cup_of_Nations_Group_C" title="2015 Africa Cup of Nations Group C">group stage</a> against <a href="/wiki/Senegal_national_football_team" title="Senegal national football team">Senegal</a> led Mahrez the national team to the quarter-finals, scoring the first goal of a match ending 20.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> then against <a href="/wiki/Ivory_Coast_national_football_team" title="Ivory Coast national football team">Ivory Coast</a> gave assists for <a href="/wiki/El_Arabi_Hillel_Soudani" class="mw-redirect" title="El Arabi Hillel Soudani">El Arabi Hillel Soudani</a> were not enough to exclude from the quarter-finals 31.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup> then in the second Round of the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_%E2%80%93_CAF_Second_Round" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification  CAF Second Round">2018 World Cup qualifier</a> against <a href="/wiki/Tanzania_national_football_team" title="Tanzania national football team">Tanzania</a> helped Mahrez in the team qualified for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_%E2%80%93_CAF_Third_Round" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification  CAF Third Round">group stage</a> where he scored a goal and assists for <a href="/wiki/Carl_Medjani" title="Carl Medjani">Carl Medjani</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Mahrez was named in coach <a href="/wiki/Georges_Leekens" title="Georges Leekens">Georges Leekens</a>' Algeria squad for the <a href="/wiki/2017_Africa_Cup_of_Nations" title="2017 Africa Cup of Nations">2017 Africa Cup of Nations</a> in Gabon.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup> In their opening game, he scored both goals in a 22 draw with <a href="/wiki/Zimbabwe_national_football_team" title="Zimbabwe national football team">Zimbabwe</a><sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> and was awarded Man of the Match.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In October 2017, with Algeria's chances of reaching the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a> already ended, Mahrez and his (at the time) Leicester teammate <a href="/wiki/Islam_Slimani" title="Islam Slimani">Islam Slimani</a> were dropped from the national team, with coach <a href="/wiki/Lucas_Alcaraz" title="Lucas Alcaraz">Lucas Alcaraz</a> selecting several new players.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> On 18 November 2018, in the <a href="/wiki/2019_Africa_Cup_of_Nations_qualification" title="2019 Africa Cup of Nations qualification">2019 Africa Cup of Nations qualifier</a> Mahrez scored a brace in a 41 away victory against <a href="/wiki/Togo_national_football_team" title="Togo national football team">Togo</a>, his first goal with the national team since <a href="/wiki/2017_Africa_Cup_of_Nations" title="2017 Africa Cup of Nations">2017 Africa Cup of Nations</a> to lead Algeria to qualify for the <a href="/wiki/2019_Africa_Cup_of_Nations" title="2019 Africa Cup of Nations">2019 Africa Cup of Nations</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In May 2019, he was named to Algeria's 23-man squad for the <a href="/wiki/2019_Africa_Cup_of_Nations" title="2019 Africa Cup of Nations">2019 Africa Cup of Nations</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup> By the decision of coach <a href="/wiki/Djamel_Belmadi" title="Djamel Belmadi">Djamel Belmadi</a>, Mahrez was chosen to be captain of Algeria at the Africa Cup of Nations.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup> Mahrez scored a 90+5 minute goal in a 21 win against <a href="/wiki/Nigeria_national_football_team" title="Nigeria national football team">Nigeria</a> in the semi-finals of the competition.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup> Later on, Algeria managed to win the tournament which was their first since 1990.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Riyad_Mahrez&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Style of play">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>A left-footed player, Mahrez usually plays as a right winger, a position which allows him to cut inside and shoot on goal with his stronger foot, or make <a href="/wiki/Cross_(football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Cross (football)">deliveries</a> into the penalty area; however, he is a versatile player, who is capable of playing anywhere across the front line, both in the <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Centre-forward" title="Forward (association football)">centre</a>, or on either flank. A quick, creative, and technically gifted player, his main traits are his trickery, balance, turn of pace, flair, and <a href="/wiki/Dribbling#Association_football" title="Dribbling">dribbling</a> skills. Although he is capable of scoring goals, he is also an excellent <a href="/wiki/Assist_(association_football)" title="Assist (association football)">assist</a> provider, courtesy of his ability to create chances for his teammates.<sup id="cite_ref-strada_95-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-strada-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup> Despite his ability, however, his record from the <a href="/wiki/Penalty_kick_(association_football)" title="Penalty kick (association football)">penalty</a> spot has been inconsistent throughout his career.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup> In his youth, he was noted for his ball skills, but was often overlooked due to his slender build;<sup id="cite_ref-doyle_7-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-doyle-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> when Quimper's youth manager Ronan Salaün and his assistant Mickaël Pellen first noticed Mahrez, they commented that he was talented, a good <a href="/wiki/Free_kick_(association_football)" title="Free kick (association football)">set-piece</a> taker, and he possessed excellent technique and dribbling skills with both feet, but that he was very slim and was lacking in the tactical aspect of the game, as he played primarily by instinct, having grown up playing <a href="/wiki/Street_football" title="Street football">street football</a>; as such, after signing him, Salaün advised Mahrez to use his intelligence to avoid challenges, as he believed that he was not strong enough to withstand physical tackles.<sup id="cite_ref-street_13-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-street-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-strada_95-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-strada-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup> Leicester's former head of recruitment, Steve Walsh noted upon observing Mahrez play that: "Riyad was a bit raw but he had a great touch. He could kill the ball dead and go past people. I liked his positivity. Some of his decision-making wasnt that great and defensively he wasnt the best, but you could see that he had real talent."<sup id="cite_ref-street_13-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-street-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> Mahrez has credited his former Leicester manager Claudio Ranieri for helping him to develop the tactical aspect of his game.<sup id="cite_ref-strada_95-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-strada-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup> During his time at Manchester City under manager Pep Guardiola, Mahrez was also able to improve his defensive skills and work-rate, as well as his decisionmaking.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup> However, Mahrez has his own special move dubbed as "La spéciale", in which he fakes a shot with his left foot, then he flicks the ball behind the right foot to dribble his opponent.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Riyad_Mahrez&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Personal life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Mahrez married his English girlfriend Rita Johal in 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-doyle_7-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-doyle-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup> Their daughter was born later that year.<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup> In June 2019, the couple, who by that time had two daughters, were ordered to pay a former nanny more than £3,600 in unpaid wages.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup> In October 2020, it was confirmed that Mahrez is now in a relationship with model Taylor Ward after splitting from Johal.<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Mahrez is a practising Muslim.<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup> In June 2017, he made the <a href="/wiki/Umrah" title="Umrah">Umrah</a> pilgrimage to <a href="/wiki/Mecca" title="Mecca">Mecca</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In May 2020, Mahrez lost hundreds of thousands of pounds worth of valuables after his penthouse apartment in Manchester was burgled.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 7 September 2020, he tested positive for COVID-19.<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career_statistics">Career statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Riyad_Mahrez&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Career statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
